Birds Eye Voila! Sweet &amp; Sour Shrimp :: Directions for Me


Directions
Keep frozen.Do not thaw.Cook thoroughly.For food safety & quality follow these instructions carefully:Keep frozen - do not thaw.Contains raw shrimp.Cook thoroughly to a temperature of 165 degrees F. Cooked shrimp will be opaque white in the center.Promptly refrigerate any leftovers.Skillet instructions (preferred method).1. Empty frozen contents of bag and sauce pouch into a 10-inch non-stick skillet.2. Cook covered over medium  high heat for 13 to 14 minutes or until heated through, stirring occasionally.3. Stir and serve.Microwave instructions:1. Empty frozen contents of bag and sauce pouch into a 2 quart microwave safe dish. Cover.2. Cook for 10 minutes, stirring halfway through.3. Stir and serve.(Product was tested using an 1100 watt microwave. Microwave ovens vary in power; adjust cooking time accordingly.)Caution: product will be hot.
